#<BL2 Cold Dead Hands>

    # BL2 Cold Dead Hands v1.0.0-prerelease
    # by Apocalyptech
    # Licensed under Public Domain / CC0 1.0 Universal
    #
    # Enemies will always drop the exact gun/shield that they were using, and
    # weapons/shields are in general not otherwise findable in the world (treasure chests,
    # for instance, will not contain guns or shields).
    #
    # In the default configuration, enemy gear is MUCH improved from stock -- you will be
    # fighting enemies with gemstones, E-Tech, and even legendaries, across all weapon
    # types.  Various options for controlling the quality of gear used by enemies (and
    # thus available to yourself) can be found below.  See the README file for full
    # details.
    #
    # This mod requires that the UCP option "Skinpool Fixes (Don't uncheck this)" is
    # enabled!  If you want to run this without UCP, make sure to at least copy that
    # category over.

    #<Main Mod (best to leave all this checked)>

        #<Disable World Weapon/Shield Drops>

            # This section disables world drops for weapons and shields, so those items will
            # only drop from what the enemies are carrying.  Rather than deleting/disabling
            # the items entirely, we're changing them to draw from an ammo/money pool so that
            # the rest of the probabilities in the pools aren't affected.
            #
            # Note that this doesn't *completely* get rid of world weapon/shield drops, but it
            # should get rid of the vast majority of them.

            #<Main Weapon/Shield-Removing Hotfixes>

                #<hotfix><key>"SparkLevelPatchEntry-ApocDisableBalanced0"</key><value>",GD_Itempools.GeneralItemPools.Pool_Gear,BalancedItems[0].ItmPoolDefinition,,ItemPoolDefinition'GD_Itempools.LootablePools.Pool_Locker_Items_CashAndAmmo'"</value><on>

            #<Level-Specific Pool Initialization>

                # These pools are used by boss enemies to provide a proper weighted equipment
                # drop, based on the user's selection in the "Bosses Use+Drop Their Unique
                # Weapons" category.  These are re-used by enemies in different levels, to
                # conserve the number of skinpools that this mod reserves.

                set GD_CustomItemPools_allium.Mercenary.AlliumXmasSkins bAutoReadyItems True 

                set GD_CustomItemPools_allium.Psycho.AlliumXmasSkins bAutoReadyItems True 

                set GD_CustomItemPools_allium.Siren.AlliumXmasSkins bAutoReadyItems True 

                set GD_CustomItemPools_allium.Soldier.AlliumXmasSkins bAutoReadyItems True 

                set GD_CustomItemPools_allium.Mercenary.AlliumXmasHeads bAutoReadyItems True 

                set GD_CustomItemPools_allium.Psycho.AlliumXmasHeads bAutoReadyItems True 

                set GD_CustomItemPools_allium.Siren.AlliumXmasHeads bAutoReadyItems True 

            #</Level-Specific Pool Initialization>

            #<Torgue DLC Pools>

                # The Torgue DLC has a complex web of equip pools already set up already,
                # for the purpose of allowing its three gangs to have different equipped
                # gear.  Rather than try to rejigger this too much, we're going to set
                # these equip pools to drop on death as well.  We're adding in launchers
                # as possible equips for them, though.  Badass gang members will be
                # changed to use our global badass equip pools.
